<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_55a41b62-aee6-4154-95d6-d005bf6b56da'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1293259969" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1293259969?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1293259969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15268743614561771129"><b> 5 EPIC stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/0FAC8726-98CE-481F-B656-20C63C681276_zpsss4hn9ep.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441556804i/16122841._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 0FAC8726-98CE-481F-B656-20C63C681276_zpsss4hn9ep.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Kim Holden knows how to hit you right in the feels with her stories. Every single time. I really thought I would be okay reading <i>Gus</i>. That there would be no tears… boy was I wrong. My emotions were working overtime while reading this, as were my tear ducts. I will say, however, that by the end, I had such a big smile on my face and my heart was filled with so much happiness, that the tears were more than worth it.<br/><br/>Aside from Kate, Gus was my favorite character in <i>Bright Side</i>. Som</span>
  <span id="freeText15268743614561771129" style="display:none"><b> 5 EPIC stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/0FAC8726-98CE-481F-B656-20C63C681276_zpsss4hn9ep.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441556804i/16122841._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0FAC8726-98CE-481F-B656-20C63C681276_zpsss4hn9ep.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Kim Holden knows how to hit you right in the feels with her stories. Every single time. I really thought I would be okay reading <i>Gus</i>. That there would be no tears… boy was I wrong. My emotions were working overtime while reading this, as were my tear ducts. I will say, however, that by the end, I had such a big smile on my face and my heart was filled with so much happiness, that the tears were more than worth it.<br><br>Aside from Kate, Gus was my favorite character in <i>Bright Side</i>. Something about this dude just made me smile. He was such a great friend to Kate and an awesome person. But Gus without Kate… he’s just not the same Gus anymore. He doesn’t feel the same. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I don’t know how to be Gus without her, dude. I’m fucking lost as shit.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> Being on tour isn’t the same. Making music isn’t the same. Nothing is the same. <br><br>Scout is a girl who comes into Gus’s life just at the right time. They are a very unlikely pair and Scout is standoffish at first. Scout and Gus end up spending a lot of time together. Gus starts to heal, to be more of himself again. Scout see’s that. At first, she wasn’t crazy about the guy. Now she see’s this fun and beautiful person he really is. <br><i>
  <blockquote>When someone initiates kindness anonymously, you know it comes from the most pure, kind-hearted part of them because they’ll probably never be singled out and thanked. It speaks to his character.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/902D7D83-AA0F-4F97-ACD9-772968145BC6_zpsbfehjcdm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441556804i/16122842._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 902D7D83-AA0F-4F97-ACD9-772968145BC6_zpsbfehjcdm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really feel like certain people come into you life for a reason. Scout and Gus came into each others life to help heal one another. They both needed each other equally. I loved these two together. I loved that Scout never was jealous about his love for his Bright Side. She and Gus were fantastic. <br><br>Any talk of Kate… I just couldn’t handle my emotions. She is one of those characters I’ll never forget. Gus was her very best friend and she loved him so much. I’m so glad he got the happy he deserved. I loved seeing all the characters from <i>Bright Side</i> make their appearances throughout this story. And it couldn’t have ended in a more perfect way! <br><br>Kim Holden writes the most beautiful, emotional and heart-wrenching stories. Her characters are so lovable and even though her books always make me cry, they also make me smile big time. They make me want to live my life to the fullest, to Do Epic every day. And that is why I love these books so much. If you haven’t read them, you’re really missing out! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/DD1E5FC0-28F2-437F-B418-870E9F7A1ED8_zpstzxcxne9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441556804i/16122843._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo DD1E5FC0-28F2-437F-B418-870E9F7A1ED8_zpstzxcxne9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15268743614561771129" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1272709508" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1272709508" />
    <a title="Seth King" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34814076-seth-king"><img alt="Seth King" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420995275p2/34814076.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1272709508?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Seth King" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Seth King" href="/user/show/34814076-seth-king">Seth King</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1272709508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10296561500146702336">Love isn’t a one-way journey. <br/><br/>Everyone likes to read about the beginning of love, the swift beautiful descent into the butterflies. We all love the meet-cute, the café flirtations, the ensuing weeks when two characters sink into love and are swept away on a road towards their inevitable white taffeta destiny. But nobody wants to talk about the wreckage, the after effects, the sorrow that can linger after love leaves. And any form of love can leave, not just romantic love. Sometimes the loss of a</span>
  <span id="freeText10296561500146702336" style="display:none">Love isn’t a one-way journey. <br /><br />Everyone likes to read about the beginning of love, the swift beautiful descent into the butterflies. We all love the meet-cute, the café flirtations, the ensuing weeks when two characters sink into love and are swept away on a road towards their inevitable white taffeta destiny. But nobody wants to talk about the wreckage, the after effects, the sorrow that can linger after love leaves. And any form of love can leave, not just romantic love. Sometimes the loss of a friend can ache just as sweetly, and hurt just as beautifully, as romantic love being yanked away by fate. Sometimes you have to push your way back out of the remnants of love, and that is where Kim Holden’s Gus comes in. Because sometimes when it all falls away and the one your heart beats for isn’t there anymore, getting yourself back into the sun can feel like pushing a boulder up a cliff. And that story isn’t for everyone. Some people want to soar up over the jagged edges of life and stay safe from heartbreak, which is totally understandable. This world is hard enough for some people. But for those who are willing to take the journey, to cry and sweat and bleed beside a good character and then be put back together and be reminded, ultimately, of what makes us alive, Gus is the perfect book for you.<br /><br />And hey: it’s also really fun! It’s got rock stars and romance and European travel and California cool and plenty of sexy times, and love, present tense! But it’s also about life and death and all the love that can bloom in between. Running under all this fun stuff, holding it all together and making the words jump off the page with crackling electric verve, is heart. Feeling. Emotion. The stuff we live for. The stuff that bubbles up from deep down. Stuff like joy and heartbreak and ecstasy and fear and all the other wild beautiful things that make us human.<br /><br />“I get to live this, for how long I have no idea, but I’m going to live and love the hell out of it.”<br /><br />In the words of Gus himself, this is all we are ensured: this moment, right now. Live and love and savor it. After all, you never know when the love will leave and you’ll have to start pushing that boulder up that cliff all over again. Enjoy the fall - God and Kim Holden know it's all we're ever really promised in this world, anyway.<br /><br />Another epic book, Kim. I will never look at a Post-It note the same again. I can't wait to see what you do next.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10296561500146702336" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1126475762" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1126475762" />
    <a title="Megan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11050821-megan"><img alt="Megan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406169068p2/11050821.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1126475762?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan" href="/user/show/11050821-megan">Megan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11050821-megan?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11050821-megan?shelf=2015-my-top-faves">2015-my-top-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11050821-megan?shelf=2015-arc">2015-arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1126475762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14166221422280540722"><b>Bright Side wasn't only my best friend; she was like my other half... the other half of my brain, the other half of my conscience, the other half of my sense of humor, the other half of my creativity, the other half of my heart. How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?</b><br/><br/>When I opened <i>Bright Side</i> I had no clue what was in store. I went in blind and came out shining.<br/>When I opened <i>Gus</i> I knew what was coming. I knew Kim would give me heart and soul. Even thoug</span>
  <span id="freeText14166221422280540722" style="display:none"><b>Bright Side wasn't only my best friend; she was like my other half... the other half of my brain, the other half of my conscience, the other half of my sense of humor, the other half of my creativity, the other half of my heart. How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?</b><br /><br />When I opened <i>Bright Side</i> I had no clue what was in store. I went in blind and came out shining.<br />When I opened <i>Gus</i> I knew what was coming. I knew Kim would give me heart and soul. Even though I knew Gus would break my heart, I knew the path in front of him would gut me. I knew my emotions would be on my sleeve.<br />After <i>Bright Side</i> I undoubtedly knew one thing, Gus would be <b>EPIC.</b><br /><i> <br />It was.<br />He was.<br />It<b> so</b> was.</i><br /><br />The sweet and sorrowful journey of deep pain and sadness, the yearning for what's on the other side. The want to be "that" Gus again. Gus was a favorite character in my favorite Bright orange book. He was lost and broken. Just as we all suspected. Just as we all <i>were</i>. The mountainous hill Gus traveled in the beginning was where I felt the most melancholy. His choices paved a grim road. He wasn’t himself. He wasn’t our Gus. <i>Her Gus.</i> He was just there. I had to bite my tongue and hope he would see his other side. <br /> <br /><b>Yeah, in another month, I'll still be in this sinking ship. It's going down fast. I feel sorry for the rest of them because this sonofabitch doesn't even have life preservers.<br /><br />Alone. I think that's what bothers me most about losing Bright Side. With her I was never alone. Even when she lived hundreds of miles away, I was never alone.</b><br /><br />The awesome way Kim writes day to day really puts the reader in the hell Gus is in. The mourning. The sorrow. The bad choices. The conflict. Then someone so NOT wanted is in the picture and I can’t tell you how relieved I was so see a pea size piece of light. Gah, I don’t even know what to say exactly about this character because it isn’t fair to YOU to spoil it. But I loved the LONG growth these two characters traveled. There wasn’t any quick perfection here. It was work. It was hard. But it was beautiful to watch. The gain both received is well worth the enormous amount of pain they had to hurdle over. They strengthen in a very unorthodox way but for them it’s what needed to happen. Mentally these two bonded over old fashion friendship. Which enhanced my fall for them. <br /><br /><b>I haven't written like that since Bright Side was around. I always feel her in my heart these days, because that's where she lives. I walk around with her inside me every day. And it doesn't hurt anymore.<br /> The presence I felt tonight wasn't internal. It was physical. Tangible. Like someone was in the room with me, feeding me. Little did I know, she was just on the other side of the door. Filling my soul.</b><br /><br />Just as the title says Gus; this was certainly all about him, it was about Bright Side.<br /><br /><i>Katie.</i><br /><br />God, so much Katie. Anytime she was mention or just thought about my throat closed up and my heart raced. We were able to get a glimpse into many characters we fell hard for. Two in particularly. I loved what we had but heavens above I could have had more. So much more. <br /><br /> <b>"I miss Katie, Gus. And I'll always love her. Not a day goes by that I don't think about her. It's not pain; it's joy. I'm living my life for her. I have no intention of wasting it."</b><br /><br />Final thoughts: You won’t be disappointed. You will feel and break. That’s guaranteed. But come the end you will have no disappointments. This was another EPIC book by one totally EPIC author. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14166221422280540722" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1131577998" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1131577998" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1131577998?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131577998" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13254381330480831313"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Bright Side wasn’t only my best friend; she was like my other half… the other half of my brain, the other half of my conscience, the other half of my sense of humor, the other half of my creativity, the other half of my heart. How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Kim Holden delivered a sequel that for me was much more creative and less predictable than it’s predecessor. To be honest, I was in moderate like with the first bo</span>
  <span id="freeText13254381330480831313" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Bright Side wasn’t only my best friend; she was like my other half… the other half of my brain, the other half of my conscience, the other half of my sense of humor, the other half of my creativity, the other half of my heart. How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Kim Holden delivered a sequel that for me was much more creative and less predictable than it’s predecessor. To be honest, I was in moderate like with the first book but in this book I <b>FELT</b> Kate’s importance in Gus’ life, in his heart and in his soul. Gus is lost without Bright Side just broken and and he stumbling along his band’s tour dates under a haze of woman and alcohol. <br> <br><b>
  <i>“Alone. I think that's what bothers me most about losing Bright Side. With her I was never alone. Even when she lived hundreds of miles away, I was never alone.”</i>
</b><br><br>Scout MacKenzie is hired to join the tour and her and Gus maintain a barely there friendship but Gus sets his mother up with a new assistant and so when the tour is over Scout ends up working for Gus’ wonderful mother, Audrey. <br><br>Scout and Gus’ love story itself is very slow paced (no instant love however I wanted some sparks and more butterfly moments than the slow burn- thus not a full 5 Star) but their relationship did progress realistically and not in an aggravating way. Scout’s prior relationship and past play a part in her “Impatient” and shy persona.<br><br><b>
  <i>”People I love don’t know how to love me back. They hurt me. That’s how they love. That’s how they love.”</i>
</b><br><br>The story catches a reader up with all the cast of the first book including Keller and sweet little Stella. I found that although Kate wasn’t in this book she was in each and every page in such a lovely profound way. The author truly did a wonderful job writing this story it had heart, originality and hope. <br><br><b>
  <i>”My heart is big enough for both of them. Bright Side helped make me the man I am, and Scout helped me remember who that man was, helping me become my own person.”</i>
</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13254381330480831313" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1401630083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17703681889292877198"><b> 4.5 stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/gus%20collage.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443414955i/16358475._SX540_.png' alt=' photo gus collage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>***Warning, there will be spoilers in this review for those of you who haven't read Bright Side yet, so only read on if you have read Bright Side or are fine with spoilers. I warned you!!!***<br/><br/>Gus was a book I was hesitant to read as Bright Side shattered my heart. I HATE unrequited love and I cried so hard for Gus at the end of that book for being in love with a girl who he didn't get a chance a</span>
  <span id="freeText17703681889292877198" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/gus%20collage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443414955i/16358475._SX540_.png" alt=" photo gus collage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>***Warning, there will be spoilers in this review for those of you who haven't read Bright Side yet, so only read on if you have read Bright Side or are fine with spoilers. I warned you!!!***<br><br>Gus was a book I was hesitant to read as Bright Side shattered my heart. I HATE unrequited love and I cried so hard for Gus at the end of that book for being in love with a girl who he didn't get a chance at forever with. So this book begins with Gus as an absolute wreck at the beginning. He's on tour just after Kate's death and he's not handling it well at all. Losing himself in drinking, drugs and women he can barely function as a normal person throughout the day. It's on this tour where Gus meets Scout, the personal assistant hired by his asshole boss. Scout is not impressed with Gus and his behavior, and she also doesn't know why he's acting this way so she sees him as a stereotypical rock star. Gus sees Scout as uptight, and even calls her Impatient because she's barely patient with him.<br><br><b> <i> “Some people wear their scars on the outside. Others wear them on the inside. Same difference. Your character, your heart, your essence, that’s what’s important, because that’s the real you. All the rest, our looks, the material stuff? It's just meaningless bullshit.” </i> </b><br><br>As the tour continues, the two strike up a tentative friendship but nothing more. Gus's mom needs a new PA and Gus manages to get Scout the job. When he returns from the tour he discovers his mother let Scout stay with them in her house until she's saved up enough for her own place. Scout begins to see that Gus is actually a really great guy, that he was just going through something horrible at the time. Slowly Gus begins to live life without Bright Side haunting him.<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421135336i/13327545.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>While this book brought tears to my eyes, it was a hell of a lot easier to read than Bright Side was. I still have a hard time with that book, mostly because I cannot stand unhappy endings. This book was Gus's redemption, his second life without his childhood sweetheart. Over time Gus was able to look back on Kate with happiness and not sadness. I loved the bromance between Gus and Keller; instead of resenting each other they chose to bond over their love of the same woman. <br><br><b> <i> “You only get one chance at this circus called life. Don’t sit in the crowd watchin’ it happen. You jump right in and be the ringleader. That’s where you find your fire.” </i> </b><br><br>I really liked Scout. She wasn't the polar opposite of Kate, but I appreciated that she wasn't the most positive person. Not that she was negative, she just saw life differently because of everything that happened to her. She hid so people wouldn't see her scars, physical and emotional ones. The weight of the world was on her shoulders but she didn't break, she just kept going and working hard.<br><br>I loved Scout and Gus together, the sticky notes scenes were among my favorites. The romance was a very slow burn and it worked for this book. No instalove, the two got to know each other before diving in. And it made it that much more special of a relationship when they did because it was something great that evolved into something even more wonderful. <br><br>I also want to mention what an amazing writer Kim Holden is. The entire book flowed so well, there wasn't any moments where I skimmed or thought was awkward plot wise. Gus was an easy going guy, and the writing style fit with him. Low angst for those of you angst allergic out there. I expected a little bit of drama of Scout being in Kate's shadow but that never happened and I'm glad, it would have never worked for the main characters if Scout didn't feel secure in her relationship with Gus. She knew Kate was a part of what made him who he was and she embraced that instead of fearing it.<br><br>So it was easier to rate this book than the first. I'm so happy Kim Holden decided to write this book and give us Gus. If you loved the first book or wanted closure, this is the book for you!<br><br><b> <i> “I think people find each other when they’re ready for them. When they need each other the most. And it’s in that time of need that the strongest relationships are formed.” </i> </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17703681889292877198" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1752111710" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1752111710?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Bright Side fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=fuck-buddy-read">fuck-buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=family-friendship">family-friendship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=athlete-artiste">athlete-artiste</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1752111710" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15363893831914765457"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Book 2 of 2 from Bright Side series<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473578595i/20484356.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Gustov (Gus) Hawthorne took the loss of his best friend hard. He lost one thing that tethered him to the ground. Without it, he quickly spiraled down to self-destruction. As lead singer and guitarist of the now popular band Rook, he was supposed to be their leader, but his detachment forced the record label to have someone keep close eyes on the band.<br/><br/>Scout MacKenzie was necessary addition to Rook</span>
  <span id="freeText15363893831914765457" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Book 2 of 2 from Bright Side series<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473578595i/20484356.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gustov (Gus) Hawthorne took the loss of his best friend hard. He lost one thing that tethered him to the ground. Without it, he quickly spiraled down to self-destruction. As lead singer and guitarist of the now popular band Rook, he was supposed to be their leader, but his detachment forced the record label to have someone keep close eyes on the band.<br><br>Scout MacKenzie was necessary addition to Rook camp. As their PA, her job was to make sure everything went smooth. Other than that, she kept her distance and avoid unnecessary contact. But her kindness to Gus didn't go unnoticed and he was determined to break her shell while mending his own heart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I absolutely love Gus in Bright Side. He was the best thing about that book and the reason why I kept putting this off for so long. I was afraid the possibility of not loving it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>And when he sings, I'm drowning. Drowning in the depths of the emotion pouring out of him.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Gus was epic in Bright Side. I could feel his heart and his passion on that one. Unfortunately I felt a lot less in his own book. I love seeing his struggles but it wasn't as intense as I wanted it to be. I wanted to see him goes from the depth of hell and soar up like a Phoenix. He did that, I just needed it to be on max level lol!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473578595i/20484357.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Scout or Impatient as Gus called her was a good match to Gus. Her reserved personality complemented his outgoing one. I like how they pushed each other to rise above their own issues.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Bright Side helped make me the man I am, and Scout helped me remember who that man was, helping me become my own person.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book is more of friendship than love story. The romance was slow burn which I don't mind but there were parts where the plot progressed was too slow pace for my liking. Also, it's inevitable that Kate overshadowed Scout.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>"I showed you a different side of me tonight. It's your turn."</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Gus is a story of a man rediscovering himself and his passion for music and life after losing his heart. The slow burn romance would remind readers you could always come back after a fall.<br><br><i><b>Note 1:</b><br>When a book ends a certain way, I always prefer it to stay that way, because it is hard to find a sequel that is worthy of the original. But that's just me because I have a specific need when it comes to my reading lol! With that said, I don't regret reading this one and I will always love Bright Side Gus :D </i><br><br><i><b>Note 2:</b><br>They communicate using sticky notes, thus the sticky notes in my teasers lol!</i><br><br><br><b>Books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22669832.Bright_Side__Bright_Side___1_" title="Bright Side (Bright Side, #1) by Kim Holden" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1404654413s/22669832.jpg" alt="Bright Side (Bright Side, #1) by Kim Holden" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23389993.Gus__Bright_Side___2_" title="Gus (Bright Side, #2) by Kim Holden" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1430743077s/23389993.jpg" alt="Gus (Bright Side, #2) by Kim Holden" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><b>☘ ♢ ☘ . . . (F)BR With Mercedes . . . ☘ ♢ ☘</b><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454304059i/17942101.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1896927244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17958575700361840854"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478196754i/21045815.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478196754i/21045816.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>➦Good book! Unfortunately, just like with the first book in this series, I couldn't quite connect with the characters all the way. I loved Gus, the hero. I like the heroine. But I just never quite fell in love with them as a couple. <br/><br/>➦May be it was the whole "dead ex" thing. Ok, she wasn't his ex but he was deeply in love with her. Normally stuff like this wouldn't bother me but I felt like the bringing up of Bright Side was constant and kept taking away from the romance. At least for me... There</span>
  <span id="freeText17958575700361840854" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478196754i/21045815.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478196754i/21045816.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>➦Good book! Unfortunately, just like with the first book in this series, I couldn't quite connect with the characters all the way. I loved Gus, the hero. I like the heroine. But I just never quite fell in love with them as a couple. <br><br>➦May be it was the whole "dead ex" thing. Ok, she wasn't his ex but he was deeply in love with her. Normally stuff like this wouldn't bother me but I felt like the bringing up of Bright Side was constant and kept taking away from the romance. At least for me... There was just... too much. I wanted to move on faster.<br><br>➦Speaking of faster. I am a fan of slow burn. But it has to be done in a way that doesn't make me want to fast forward through pages and pages. Descriptions of lives of secondary characters? Not a fan of. Like, I don't really care about how your friends who you see once a year are doing: where they work, what they plan to do in the future. This bear is running out of patience.<br><br>➦I did, for the most part, enjoy Gus' journey of healing and acceptance. I just wished he would throw a bone to the heroine once in a while. This slow burn was slow. Just when I think the tho main characters will be thrown in a situation where they will get some sharing to do (or at the very least spending time together) the story takes a detour somewhere. gurr T.T This one wasn't entirely for me.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477941105i/21012016.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1289564820" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1289564820" />
    <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance"><img alt="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481665315p2/10247668.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1289564820?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=books-that-make-me-feel-and-cry">books-that-make-me-feel-and-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=top-favourite-reads-of-all-time">top-favourite-reads-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=2015-favourite-reads">2015-favourite-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=need-more-than-five-stars">need-more-than-five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1289564820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11890329998851932004"><b>5+++++ Heal my Heart Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/E3669D9A-3B0A-4A51-BC1F-A225E57C2AC9_zpshozjvanq.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432906636i/15019467._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo E3669D9A-3B0A-4A51-BC1F-A225E57C2AC9_zpshozjvanq.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/>If any of you are worried to delve into this after Bright Side, I'll just say that this book gives us the happy feeling. It will give you everything and more, I'm telling you, I am very happy with how this book unfolded and ended for me its was the best way for Kim to help us readers to move on and ultimately again to question ourselves. To think and then to understand who Gus really is. It still has emotional moments but its not gut wrenching just happiness <b> for m</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11890329998851932004" style="display:none"><b>5+++++ Heal my Heart Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/E3669D9A-3B0A-4A51-BC1F-A225E57C2AC9_zpshozjvanq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432906636i/15019467._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo E3669D9A-3B0A-4A51-BC1F-A225E57C2AC9_zpshozjvanq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>If any of you are worried to delve into this after Bright Side, I'll just say that this book gives us the happy feeling. It will give you everything and more, I'm telling you, I am very happy with how this book unfolded and ended for me its was the best way for Kim to help us readers to move on and ultimately again to question ourselves. To think and then to understand who Gus really is. It still has emotional moments but its not gut wrenching just happiness <b> for me anyway</b>. This book was heart warming had moments that included Kate and all that surrounded her but above all it's a story about family and friendship. <br> <br><b>So What's it about</b><br>So if you've read Bright Side you know that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Gus lost his other half his best friend and the love of his life <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> . Hence the reckless way he is living life on the road <b>AT ALL</b> he's away from home and he's away from his Ma and is grieving over his other half The first 1/4 I would say is the hardest to read because Gus isn't his usually happy go lucky self, he's going down the path of self destruction which included booze, drugs and women. That's what his life pretty much entailed. Drowning his sorrows and Running away from his problems and those aspects just were there to stop him <b>remembering about HER.</b> <br> <br>But then things change and he meets Scout she's there to be his 'Babysitter' because the band and organisers of the Tour can't handle him anymore . He gets someone to deal with him and everything that he needs, unlucky for both sides they both aren't greatly happy about the job. <br>Scout is a quiet nonsense kind of gal, she doesn't take shit from Gus , and at the same time doesn't get too involved with him. She has her own issues she's dealing with and needs this job opportunity so she is basically there to help but not to feel. Saying that Gus has a way to help her even if he doesn't want to, Scout at the beginning I would say is a buffer that helps Gus to breathe a little easier she's a deterrent in his darkness and that just helps him gradually to start to live again. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/E993CDF2-AF45-4FCB-90EC-8954BC0AFB55_zpsn1rhcchv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432762963i/15004726._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo E993CDF2-AF45-4FCB-90EC-8954BC0AFB55_zpsn1rhcchv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Even though they both don't want to be around each other greatly there were some funny moments. Things I enjoyed about this part was Gus's dry sense of humour and likewise how Scout mothered him to you know 'Have a shower' or when your clothes don't move <b>It's time to wash them.... it's time</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>Sometimes you meet people and you know the meeting wasn't chance. That they need you or you need them, sometimes both. </b>
</blockquote> <br>Over time they both start to see a different side to each other and that alone opens up there friendship, it helps them both breathe. It helps them to see how to live again. Then when the Tour ends Scout gets a position working with Gus's Ma and in that they both continue to see each other daily. Scout starts to see who Gus really is in the comfort of his home; the bubbly happy go lucky guy . he is the Gus who puts himself last in every obstacle and always one step ahead in being there for everyone around him, <b>he's the Jedi of friendship</b> you just can't help but fall for his character and who is resembles. <br> <br>Kim deliver's another heart warming story that seeps into your pours and gradually see the family theme in this story. There are a few new characters to enjoy too....<br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/Gus_zpsvkgrp08n.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432906636i/15019469._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Gus_zpsvkgrp08n.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Characters that make him start to believe in himself, characters where I would say bright Side put there for him on purpose. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/E7A68EA0-0E13-4070-803D-6700686D5874_zpsm3bqyv3e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432906636i/15019470._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo E7A68EA0-0E13-4070-803D-6700686D5874_zpsm3bqyv3e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Kim has a way with words that make you as a reader <b>FEEL</b>In the quiet moments I really did see what Kim was doing as I read his story, this wasn't just a romance but a book on new beginnings and life. Gus learned how to be himself again and even more so he learnt how to give freely to the people around him who needed him and who plainly just wanted him to be there and around them because his nature was just an all around existence of <b>love.</b> <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/BB9BEBDD-5902-4787-AF96-1C145B3544F8_zpsap7qqky3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432850588i/15012561._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BB9BEBDD-5902-4787-AF96-1C145B3544F8_zpsap7qqky3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>I'm not going to say anything else other than this book is Deep, Hard, Intense, Emotional and then Loving, Honest, and Heart Warming. This is a book of LOVE and honest to God this book has all the FEELS people just need to give these characters a chance, I know some don't like NA reads for immaturity and the age limits of the characters but this book is about Family and living its a story about learning how to live, how to continue and how to move forward. But above all this book is Simplicity Kims books to talk to my heart in a way that speaks volumes, it touched me in ways I can't express but this book is an <b>EXPERIENCE</b> that everyone needs to try whatever age you are (Just my opinion though). <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/86FBDACA-7245-486E-8271-F51600C259D3_zpsq48tisf1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432906636i/15019471._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 86FBDACA-7245-486E-8271-F51600C259D3_zpsq48tisf1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>The Music</b><br>Again the music was apart of the story as much as the words were it was the life of the book so I'd highly recommend you listening some of these tracks as you read the book. <br> <br>I Hope You Suffer ~ AFI <br>I Need My Girl ~ The National<br>Cope ~ Manchester Orchestra<br>Me ~ The 1975<br>Killing You ~ Broods <br>Figure It Out ~ Royal Blood<br>The Scientist ~ Coldplay<br>Homesick ~ Catfish and the Bottlemen <br>Baby Please Don't Leave me ~ Buddy Guy<br>Love Me Like You Used To ~ You Ask Me At Six<br>Giants ~ Bear Hands<br>All Around me ~ Flyleaf<br>Tiny Raindrop ~ Balance and Composure<br>Fall into the Party ~ Twin Atlantic<br>Kiss Me ~ Ed Sheeran<br> <br><b>This book was written for the READERS so READ IT!!!!</b> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/38597339-A121-414A-92DC-CAF3BA1A93DC_zpsxpumqdw9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432906636i/15019472._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 38597339-A121-414A-92DC-CAF3BA1A93DC_zpsxpumqdw9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>That. Is. All.</b><br><br><b>For more Reviews and Blog Posts</b><br><a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1342643326" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1342643326" />
    <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword"><img alt="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603584262p2/28146945.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1342643326?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword">Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25571652-gus">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=character-driven-story">character-driven-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=favorites-2018">favorites-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=loved-the-writing">loved-the-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=best-book-dedications">best-book-dedications</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=best-reviews">best-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=gave-me-butterflies">gave-me-butterflies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1342643326" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11336441195213287940"><b>4.5 “GUS” Stars</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i>”I think we were meant from the very beginning. Maybe it was all the fucking sticky notes”<br/>“You love my sticky notes.”<br/>“I do. The tour bus won’t be the same without you and your sticky notes.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>➽<u>
  <b>FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED:</b>
</u><br/><br/><b>I AM SO EMOTIONALLY INVESTED WITH THESE CHARACTERS.</b><br/><br/>How can I explain my love for this book? Is not exactly because this books is a complete masterpiece, is definitely not. Someone even wrote in a review that we just loved this book because of the existence of Bri</span>
  <span id="freeText11336441195213287940" style="display:none"><b>4.5 “GUS” Stars</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>”I think we were meant from the very beginning. Maybe it was all the fucking sticky notes”<br>“You love my sticky notes.”<br>“I do. The tour bus won’t be the same without you and your sticky notes.”</i>
</blockquote><br>➽<u>
  <b>FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED:</b>
</u><br><br><b>I AM SO EMOTIONALLY INVESTED WITH THESE CHARACTERS.</b><br><br>How can I explain my love for this book? Is not exactly because this books is a complete masterpiece, is definitely not. Someone even wrote in a review that we just loved this book because of the existence of Bright Side. It didn’t offend me because honestly I think is 100% truth. I connected and craved this story because I was a fan of all these characters on Bright Side. I fell in love with Gus from the first appearance he made in that book, and I always wished for his happy ending. I was immersed in this story then again not by the romance, but something more, just curiosity for this characters and love for the way Kim makes me wanna love life and appreciate people around me.<b>Her books make me want to be a better person, in all honesty.</b><br><br>Also, I love how her fangirling for sunset sons makes so many appearances in this book. Like she even said Gus was basically the characterization of Rory Williams, and I don’t complain, I loved having him in my imagination as Gus. <s>If you haven't listened to them, do it. They are awesome and so underrated.</s><br><br>Kim’s and my visualization of Gus: <br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1523127619i/25341411._SY540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Anyway, let’s move from ogling the picture to my actual review, although no hard feelings if you prefer to ogle the picture. <br><br><b>The writing</b>. More than the writing itself, I love the way Kim Holden thinks, is it weird? I mean I relate to a deep level with her characters philosophies on life and all her quotes hit home. Her stories always make me so emotional, like not only in ugly-cry mode, but just, happiness, sadness, nostalgia, awkwardness, desolation, peace. She certainly makes you go on a roller coaster.<br><br><b>The characters</b>. They are my life. Basically, these books are character-driven all the way, if you are not invested in the characters, you will not like the story. First Gus, Gus is one of my ultimate crushes, musician, good guy, emotional, funny, caring. His journey in this books is heartbreaking, we see all his stages dealing with grief and is so beautiful but heart-wrenching. I will honestly say I wasn’t that invested or connected with Scout, maybe is because I didn’t meet her in the last book, and she is also very distant in so many ways, but at the end of the novel I cared deeply. Families, omg this book made want to have families like this. These families are not conventional, but they are so loving. And I am not just talking about blood-related, I am talking about friends and new born families. One of my favorite characters all the way is Gus’s mom, she rocks. The sweetest, strongest and kindness women I have ever read about. <s>okay maybe Kate was up there with that description too.</s> The talent of Kim to make me care about the characters is just astounding, even if the characters appeared just in 3 chapters I was rooting for them, loving them. <br><br><b>Plot</b>. We basically follow the progress of the relationship between Gus and Scout but is also about their personal growth in different areas of their life. This book doesn’t have a mind fucking twist, is character focused all the way. AND I AM TOTALLY FINE WITH IT. <br><br><b>Relationship</b>. Slow burn romance, oh boy. I had completely forgotten how long it takes for our main characters to make a move, but I love it. I love to see how a relationship progresses from non-existent to small connection to full-blown sparks. And I fucking loved the sticky note play, like so cute. I will say I was missing a bit more chemistry, but I will repeat it again I don’t love this books because of the romance, which is weird for me but hey, there is always a first time.<br><br>The fucking epic quote of course:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"Bright Side helped make me the man I am, and Scout helped me remember who that man was, helping me become my own person. I love her so much."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>I love this series, and I will keep re-reading them throughout my whole life. If you haven’t picked up this book or the first book, try them please.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11336441195213287940" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1485162992" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1485162992" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1485162992?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25571652-gus">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10502567-jiana?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1485162992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2701992982620893403">I love this book <b>
  <i>so much</i>
</b> it makes my heart ache. <br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“I’m at the tipping point of a transformation that began months ago, an intentional decision put in motion. And it feels so fucking good. I’ve come to the full realization that my happiness, my life, falls squarely on my shoulders. No one’s gonna do it for it me. I’m the one who makes it or breaks it. It’s a choice. A choice that demands action in exchange for reward. Idleness and complacency lead to mediocrity. Sometimes action is really f</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText2701992982620893403" style="display:none">I love this book <b>
  <i>so much</i>
</b> it makes my heart ache. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“I’m at the tipping point of a transformation that began months ago, an intentional decision put in motion. And it feels so fucking good. I’ve come to the full realization that my happiness, my life, falls squarely on my shoulders. No one’s gonna do it for it me. I’m the one who makes it or breaks it. It’s a choice. A choice that demands action in exchange for reward. Idleness and complacency lead to mediocrity. Sometimes action is really fucking hard fought, but that’s when the payoff’s the highest. That’s when great things happen. Not good things … but epic things. And I’ve fallen in love with epic. It’s the only way to live.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />I read book one, Bright Side, this past summer and it basically destroyed me. Gus was one of the main characters in Bright Side and I fell for him. With the way things ended in Bright Side, I needed to read Gus's story. I love Gus so much and how he reacted to what happened in Bright Side broke my heart. This book is Gus's story (obviously). I needed to see how Gus heals and deals with his pain. I needed my baby to find happiness again. I was also scared to start this book. I knew what was coming, I knew I'd read about a broken Gus. I knew there was going to be a lot of mention of Kate. Was I ready? Yes and no. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“How do you back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever?”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />The book starts with a devastated Gus. His life literally fell apart and he simply doesn't want to survive anymore. Kim Holden is a brilliant writer. How she described Gus's suffering, sorrow and pain... it hit me right in my heart. She perfectly conveyed his emotions. I just sat there sobbing over him. After reaching his lowest point, Gus slowly starts to pick himself back up again. The healing process was super realistic and spot-on. I applaud Kim Holden for that. Gus is a beautiful character and he is easily one of my all-time favorites. His relationship with his mother and his band mates is great and I just... wow. <b>I just love Gus, okay.</b><br /><br />Scout is a new addition in the book. She's a wonderful character, as well, and I love her. <b>One thing I absolutely loved about this book was that there was <u>no insta-love</u>.</b> It's a slow burn and Scout and Gus's relationship takes time to develop and grow. It's healthy, beautiful and it's realistic. I loved it. I can't remember the last time I read a romance book with no insta-love. Round of applause for Kim Holden.<br /><br />Keller makes an appearance in this book and I loved seeing him heal, too. Keller and Gus's friendship is another beautiful thing in this book. <b>This book is just beautiful. Beautifully painful and just beautiful. Everything about it was brilliant.</b><br /><br />I cried so many times reading this. Every reminder and mention of Kate had me bawling. Gus's pain had me bawling. Keller's pain had me bawling. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“There’s something epic that happens every day if you look hard enough for it. And every day is a chance to go out there and do epic. The key is putting forth the effort.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I adore this book. It has a lot of messages - most we've heard multiple times before, but the way they were conveyed... through which characters they were conveyed... <u>that</u> makes it different. This is an unforgettable book. I highly recommend it, but definitely read Bright Side before, because this one is a sequel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2701992982620893403" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1085153123" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1085153123" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1085153123?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1085153123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13573366671319537618">Every since that heartbreaking ending and what Gus did in <i>Bright Side</i>, I've been <i>dying</i> to hear his story and thankfully, now we get to. It was really easy to like Gus in <i>Bright Side</i> and not only like him but commiserate with him. I not only wanted him to have a HEA but I <i>needed</i> it. <br/><br/>The one thing that surprised me was I had no idea how much <i>more</i> I would come to love Gus but...that comes later. First, we have to watch him self destruct. Luckily, it wasn't as bad as it could've been...thank goodnes</span>
  <span id="freeText13573366671319537618" style="display:none">Every since that heartbreaking ending and what Gus did in <i>Bright Side</i>, I've been <i>dying</i> to hear his story and thankfully, now we get to. It was really easy to like Gus in <i>Bright Side</i> and not only like him but commiserate with him. I not only wanted him to have a HEA but I <i>needed</i> it. <br><br>The one thing that surprised me was I had no idea how much <i>more</i> I would come to love Gus but...that comes later. First, we have to watch him self destruct. Luckily, it wasn't as bad as it could've been...thank goodness for Franco or it would've been much worse. <br><br>And then there's Scout...and her baggage. At first, I wasn't too happy about that. It took time away from Gus but as the story progress, it made more sense and especially with them needing and helping each other. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441499351ra/16116217.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I LOVED the sticky notes and how they were each always looking out for the other. And as much as I enjoyed the two of them together...they were really only part of the story. <br><br>The rest is, well, all the rest. All the rest of this mismatched, patched together, ragtag group that just is simply <i>family</i>. KH really had everyone come together so smoothly and so necessarily. Just like Rook's music...they all flowed together seamlessly...even Spare Ribs! <br><br>But that's the most I'm going to tell you. I can't do it justice and I don't want to. You really need to read it for yourself and see how all the pieces come together. If you read <i>Bright Side</i>, you owe it to yourself to read this. Enjoy!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431147240i/14796042.jpg" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>The Good Stuff:</u>
</b><br><br><b>Dual Pov's?</b> Yes. <br><br><b>Steam Factor? (Scale 1 - 5)</b> 3-4...Gus is really swoony! <br><br><b>Angst? (Scale 1 - 5)</b> 2-3 maybe. There's some bittersweet moments so more emotional than angsty. <br><br><b>Next book?</b> I think that's it? I couldn't find anything else at this time but I could definitely see her writing more. Maybe a spin off for Franco? or Paxton? or (gasp!) Keller? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431147288i/14796051.jpg" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432497321i/14972659.jpg" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "Nothing goes better with crackers and PB than grape juice."<br><br>♥ "I have a feeling your heart is heavy, and when your heart is heavy, everything’s harder. Dealing with life is harder. Believe me, I know. The negative is amplified, and sometimes that extinguishes the peace.”<br><br>♥ “Spare Ribs is a righteous name. And she’s no lady, Impatient. Don’t let her fool you, she’s a hardcore hustler.”<br><br>♥ “That’s the secret. You find what you love and you go for it. Life ain’t about coasting. It’s about pushin’ the damn gas pedal all the way to the floor. Same goes for fun and love, no coasting. Pedal to the floor.”<br><br>♥ "No worries. A Stella ambush is the best kind of ambush."<br><br>♥ "I won't pry, but I will supply."<br><br>♥ "But I just want tonight to be about us and this insane, unstoppable need I have to be near you. Around you. To be your friend. To make you smile. To make you laugh. To make you happy. To protect you."<br><br>♥ “You’re my everything, Scout. <i>Everything</i>. I love you with everything that I am. Everything I’ll ever be. You’re my future, sweetheart.”<br><br><br><i>(Prior to review)</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/650228.gif" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>OMG!!<b> <s>its coming out in 16 days! <b>IM READING IT! </b></s> She did Gus proud!</b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13573366671319537618" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1833722506" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1833722506" />
    <a title="Pam Nelson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15402332-pam-nelson"><img alt="Pam Nelson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544491116p2/15402332.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1833722506?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam Nelson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam Nelson" href="/user/show/15402332-pam-nelson">Pam Nelson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/31205092-gus">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=heavy-issues">heavy-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=_finished-2017">_finished-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=favorite-books-or-series">favorite-books-or-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=audiobook-club">audiobook-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15402332-pam-nelson?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1833722506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6619807443868348535">I re read because well GUS was my favorite book of 2016 and Franco audiobook just came out and I wanted to read GUS again.. <3 Loved it soooooo hard.. <br/><br/>5 Gus Stars <br/><br/>I am going to be completely honest, I wasn't going to read Gus, and here is why.   <span id="freeText6619807443868348535" style="display:none">I re read because well GUS was my favorite book of 2016 and Franco audiobook just came out and I wanted to read GUS again.. &lt;3 Loved it soooooo hard.. <br /><br />5 Gus Stars <br /><br />I am going to be completely honest, I wasn't going to read Gus, and here is why. I was completely gutted with Bright Side. Like my heart hurt too much to revisit any part of this story again. But with the coaxing of some fabulous, book friends. I decided what the heck give Gus a shot. <br /><br />And thank god I did, his book really does help heal the whole your heart will have after that book. <br />Gus has a hard time as would anyone who loses someone, and he learns to live again. It’s a brilliant story and again I am so so glad I read it. Sooooo if you tackle the Bright Side.. Read GUS afterwards. I promise the hurt won’t be has hard after him. <br /><br />*You don't have to like my review but its 100% my opinion, and I am allowed to have it.*</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1312893206?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="BabyBeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="BabyBeth" href="/user/show/41044235-babybeth">BabyBeth</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41044235-babybeth?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>
