        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1312893206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6508864782780815348">Excuse me, but NO.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396909ra/765452.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've read Bright Side and absolutely loved it. I was looking forward to seeing how Gus moves on after book one. When I read BS I had a feeling Gus was going to make a perfect book boyfriend. Kim Holden's characters are refreshing, because she writes perfectly cute, nice and feel-good characters and the men are not as*holes. But I have to say, I kinda' think all those 5 star reviews GUS has been receiving is due to the fact people still love and rave about Bright Side. Here's wh</span>
  <span id="freeText6508864782780815348" style="display:none">Excuse me, but NO.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396909ra/765452.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've read Bright Side and absolutely loved it. I was looking forward to seeing how Gus moves on after book one. When I read BS I had a feeling Gus was going to make a perfect book boyfriend. Kim Holden's characters are refreshing, because she writes perfectly cute, nice and feel-good characters and the men are not as*holes. But I have to say, I kinda' think all those 5 star reviews GUS has been receiving is due to the fact people still love and rave about Bright Side. Here's why GUS just didn't work for me:<br><br>1. The whole relationship with Scout was off. Scout wasn't a likeable character (even less so compared to the pretty perfect Kate in Bright Side). She was boring, annoying and pretty much a b*tch 70% of the book. The relationship between Gus and Scout didn't take off for a very long time and then was rushed the last 20% or so. I did NOT appreciate that.<br><br>2. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Gus was doing the usual heartbroken thing where you drink yourself to death/do drugs/ have sex with lots of random girls like every rock star experiencing grief. It was very unoriginal and I was quite surprised considering the freshness BS brought with it.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>3. Wow, the book was SLOW. I mean, BS took time to pick up speed, but I still enjoyed the journey. Gus, on the other hand, became interesting toward the 80% mark, and I almost DNFed it because of it. It was totally underwhelming and I found myself skimming a lot of parts. I think it's the author's thing, to pick up speed toward the end, and trust me, I don't really mind that at all, but NOTHING happened until we hit the 75% point. FRUSTRATING.<br><br>4. Gus came off as too nice. If you read the book you know what I mean. He was all heart. He missed an edge. I liked him better with the mystery of BS.<br><br>5. The plot was a MESS. I mean, really, a big, freaking mess. Characters came and went <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ whatever happened to that old lady he went to bingo with? There was no point to their relationship but it took like, three chapters off the book or something <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I had a feeling the characters were not making progress in their journey toward happiness. I dunno, it seemed...contrived.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434812911ra/15265538.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One last note:<br><br>I love Kim Holden's writing. I still need to write a review for BS because it was an easy 4 star book for me. But I gotta' say, this was very underwhelming and when I saw the sick average of 4.68 stars for this book I was shocked. It really didn't work for me, but maybe it's just me. Lookign forward to reading what else this author has in store for me...but Gus, baby, it's not me, it's you :(<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1620196974" />

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth Hudspeth" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth">Beth Hudspeth</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1620196974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1629588818300606094">Reviewed by: <a>Hello Beautiful Book Blog</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Perfect sequel to Bright Side. This book will help you heal and provide happiness and closure.</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>*****Spoilers for Bright Side#1 below*****</b><br/><br/><br/>Kim Holden has a way with creating the best chemistry between all of her characters. I'm not just talking about romantic chemistry, but also the friendships the characters share. It is really something special and I feel it each time I read one of her books. Just as in Bright Side, Gus is strongly character driven. I rea</span>
  <span id="freeText1629588818300606094" style="display:none">Reviewed by: <a>Hello Beautiful Book Blog</a><br><br><b>
  <i>Perfect sequel to Bright Side. This book will help you heal and provide happiness and closure.</i>
</b><br><br><b>*****Spoilers for Bright Side#1 below*****</b><br><br><br>Kim Holden has a way with creating the best chemistry between all of her characters. I'm not just talking about romantic chemistry, but also the friendships the characters share. It is really something special and I feel it each time I read one of her books. Just as in Bright Side, Gus is strongly character driven. I really value a book that makes me feel like the characters are old friends. It's a wonderful thing. Number one thing for me is the likability of the characters and as I've stated before, these are top notch.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Bright Side wasn’t only my best friend; she was like my other half ... the other half of my brain, the other half of my conscience, the other half of my sense of humor, the other half of my creativity, the other half of my heart.”</i>
</blockquote><br>I absolutely love Gus' character! He is so purely good to his core. I guess I just have a weakness for nice. I mean he's been through a lot obviously and made some bad decisions, but is healing. Reading through the process of Gus' grief helped me get through the emotions I was feeling about Kate. Every time Kate was brought up tears just filled my eyes, but by the end they were happy tears thinking about what great books these are. I am so happy I decided to give these a chance. I won't ever regret reading them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You only get one chance at this circus called life. Don’t sit in the crowd watchin’ it happen. You jump right in and be the ringleader. That’s where you find your fire.”</i>
</blockquote><br><b>Rook on the road</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462544202i/19011650.jpg" alt=" photo ontheroadrook_zpsg4paw2ci.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Scout</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462544202i/19011651._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e2b9f50c-b6a3-4e09-8da6-e9dbba594011_zpsi7knvlia.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Scout is put into Gus' life unexpectedly, mostly to babysit him on the tour... long story. She is really standoffish and has her own issues to deal with. After the tour ends Scout gets a job with Gus' mother, Audrey, being a personal assistant since hers retired. Gus is behind it, because he is a selfless person and acts on his kindness all the time. Audrey is just an amazing person and lets Scout stay with them while she is getting on her feet. With Gus and Scout living under the same roof they spend a lot of time together. This romance was sort of a slow burn instead of an insta-love, which I thought was quite lovely. I needed Gus to be happy in his life like I need my next breath.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I think people find each other when they’re ready for them. When they need each other the most. And it’s in that time of need that the strongest relationships are formed.”</i>
</blockquote><br><b>I totally see this photo as Rook with Spare Rib, the cat Gus rescues in the shot.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462544202i/19011652._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 201dbc31-162b-4f79-b45c-0c1fe2439daa_zpsqazikbv0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved seeing all of the characters from Bright Side pop up. It was like welcoming old friends home after a long trip. I loved every one of Bright Side's friends and I'm glad they were present in this book. Especially Keller and little Stella. I needed to know how they were getting along and know they were going to be okay.<br><br>These books are very dear to my heart and the characters are as well. I won't forget this incredible journey of love, loss, and healing.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Epic is a state of mind.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462544202i/19011653._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 0dc63050-3e4b-4671-98ff-687709daa4ae_zpsw3mywcea.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>It's Showtime!</b></span>

<div id="review_1278472034" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1278472034" />
    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1278472034?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=music">music</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=book-husband">book-husband</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=book-club">book-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1278472034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12580945720289741849"><b>***** 5 <i>Wonderful</i> Stars*****</b><br/><br/><br/>This duet is very dear to my heart and I had no doubt I was going to love <i>Gus</i> as much, if not more than <i>Bright Side</i>. These are characters that stay in your heart forever, their stories, not only give you the feels but they will also inspire you to try to always live life on the bright side.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/a89cf044-11fc-43c2-ad6d-c82efd743053_zpsjbczwptu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438290459i/15690743.jpg' alt=' photo a89cf044-11fc-43c2-ad6d-c82efd743053_zpsjbczwptu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The story picks up right after Bright Side left Gus. He was completely lost without his best friend. Then he is forced to go on tour to promote his band's new album in Europe.<br/><br/>Gu</span>
  <span id="freeText12580945720289741849" style="display:none"><b>***** 5 <i>Wonderful</i> Stars*****</b><br><br><br>This duet is very dear to my heart and I had no doubt I was going to love <i>Gus</i> as much, if not more than <i>Bright Side</i>. These are characters that stay in your heart forever, their stories, not only give you the feels but they will also inspire you to try to always live life on the bright side.<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/a89cf044-11fc-43c2-ad6d-c82efd743053_zpsjbczwptu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438290459i/15690743.jpg" alt=" photo a89cf044-11fc-43c2-ad6d-c82efd743053_zpsjbczwptu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The story picks up right after Bright Side left Gus. He was completely lost without his best friend. Then he is forced to go on tour to promote his band's new album in Europe.<br><br>Gus is deep into dark times. He's using anything and anyone he can find to help him scape from the reality that it's his life, he doesn't know who he is without the girl who was his biggest support and strength. When they get back to the states, due to his bad behavior his manager finds Gus a PA, someone who can make sure he stays on his game. That person is Scout; she's not affected by Gus's looks or rockstar persona, she's focused on just getting the job done.<br><br>Scout and Gus get on wrong foot at first, they can barely stand each other. Is only when the tour is over and he suggests Scout as his mother's new Personal Assistant, that a friendship slowly starts to form. Scout realizes that she's just as lost as Gus; both of these characters are struggling to find the light at the end of the tunnel. <br><br>This book's message is kind of like that bible verse that says; <i> Love Never Fails.</i> Family, true friendship and love is what will help Gus and Scout heal and feel inspired about a bright future. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/4743950b-304b-4fbf-8b1b-8421c6e9651b_zps1lx4deal.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438290459i/15690744.jpg" alt=" photo 4743950b-304b-4fbf-8b1b-8421c6e9651b_zps1lx4deal.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kim Holden literally rocked my world with both of these books. Even though I cried a ton, after I was done reading them my heart was soaring. Filled with music and such a positive message about love, only makes me feel super happy and inspired. Absolutely beautiful read!!! <br><br>This book has an awesome music playlist at the end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12580945720289741849" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1084677161" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1084677161" />
    <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover"><img alt="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369044455p2/11672704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1084677161?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover">Donna ~ The Romance Cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover?shelf=5-star-reads-2015">5-star-reads-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084677161" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12332680209808199235">GUS (Bright Side, #2) by Kim Holden<br/>5 stars!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Grief. Anger. Grief. Anger. Grief...Anger.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>After you have read something as perfect as Bright Side you are always going to be nervous reading the sequel, I mean, how can something so perfect ever be matched or even topped? Well, I needn’t have worried at all. As soon as GUS landed on my kindle I was all in from the first to last word. Kim Holden does Gus proud in this book and she has given us a story that was honest, real, emotional, inte</span>
  <span id="freeText12332680209808199235" style="display:none">GUS (Bright Side, #2) by Kim Holden<br />5 stars!!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Grief. Anger. Grief. Anger. Grief...Anger.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />After you have read something as perfect as Bright Side you are always going to be nervous reading the sequel, I mean, how can something so perfect ever be matched or even topped? Well, I needn’t have worried at all. As soon as GUS landed on my kindle I was all in from the first to last word. Kim Holden does Gus proud in this book and she has given us a story that was honest, real, emotional, intense and so heart-breakingly genuine that you just fell in love with these characters all over again. Kim Holden has once again touched my heart, I felt it all, the grief, the desolation, the turn around, that eureka moment and all the happy that follows. This book was perfectly balanced and I was so thankful that it rang true to life, losing someone that you are extremely close too is not something that you get over easily and it was never brushed aside, it was raw, but it was perfect.<br /><br />Gus as you could imagine really struggles in the beginning and this is where I felt Kim Holden really hit her stride. As I said above, I felt his pain, I felt his emotions, and I felt his devastation. Gus really struggles to find himself. Bright Side was his other half, his soul mate, how could someone possibly go on when one half of them is missing? I have to say I was really worried about Gus, I knew that this was going to hit him hard, but to see how vulnerable and broken he was, was soul crushing at times. I always knew that he would have to hit rock bottom before he could start his painful clamour to the surface and the way this book was written made that journey all the more honest, genuine and unequivocally believable.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Bright Side wasn’t only my best friend; she was like my other half...the other half of my brain, the other half of my conscience, the other half of my sense of humour, the other half of my creativity, the other half of my heart. How do you go back to doing what you did before, when half of you is gone forever.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Gus in the beginning was a shell of the man that we loved and knew, he couldn’t write, he couldn’t play, he just existed and even then that was up for debate at times. I wanted him to watch the DVD, I wanted him to see what and who he had become, Bright Side wouldn’t have wanted this, he needed to know, he needed to be told but he just wouldn’t listen. He needed to work through his pain and even Bright Side herself had anticipated it, it just went to show how bone deep their connection was, it was beautiful. Stunningly beautiful.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I don’t know to be Gus without her, dude. I’m fucking lost as shit.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />We finally get that little sliver of light in the form of Scout, I am not going to say too much about Scout but she was the wake-up call that Gus needed. He made her life hell, but she gave back as good as she got. The journey that these two went on was honest and real, no insta love, not even instant friendship but none the less a beautiful, sometimes hilarious read that will have your emotions all over the place. In the beginning these two were by no means perfect together, but they worked, they worked well, they were just what each other needed, they were there for each other, the right place at the right time. The way Kim Holden develops their relationship before your eyes was inspiring, that character connection resonates deep within and once again we have another character that you cannot help but love.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He doesn’t live life, he feels it. I’ve seen it. I’ve seen grief strangle him. And I’ve seen happiness make him glow with a brightness so intense it’s almost blinding. That’s what makes him so special. It’s not his talent or his looks. It’s how much he feels.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Once again though Bright Side is not forgotten, this book was a celebration of her life, how life became after Bright Side but no-one would ever forget, forever at the forefront of people’s thoughts and memories and forever uttering or thinking “what would Bright Side do”? Every time she was mentioned the tears came, I just couldn’t help it and my thoughts would wander back to that orange book that decimated me last year.<br /><br />It was great to catch up with all the characters, no-body was forgotten in this book, while this book is predominantly all about Gus, Gus’s journey would never be complete without his friends and they are all there as one big happy family, even Keller. This is what I loved, Kim Holden brought them all together, they were a unit, they may have lost the anchor that held them tethered together but those friendships were for life and life means life.<br /><br />This was one emotional journey, but it was a necessary evil, the good far outweighs the bad and the journey that Kim Holden takes you on to get there was well worth the tears and the tissues. You have to sit back and salute Kim Holden, the woman is a genius, Bright Side was EPIC, Gus was EPIC, this author is just EPIC. This woman knows how to nail character connection; she brings these people to life. She knows how to nail emotions, she makes me cry even when not intended but most of all you live and breathe it all and that is what I love in a book. I want it to be an experience and this is one experience I will never ever forget. I totally and utterly loved Bright Side but I can honestly say I loved Gus just as much.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Not good things...but epic things. And I’ve fallen in love with epic. It’s the only way to live.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Amazing job Kim Holden, you should be so proud, not only did you do Gus Hawthorne justice but us the reader too. You gave us a raw, emotional, yet uplifting story that will have mended many hearts. But I can’t reiterate enough how much I respect the honesty in this book, it made it for me. It was real, it was believable, dude...it was EPIC.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theromancecover.com">www.theromancecover.com</a><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12332680209808199235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer12871595173631183449">Kim Holden....... Dude........ You totally broke my heart in the most Epic way....... AGAIN!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1368.photobucket.com/user/salomax1/media/___5295375_orig_zpsklwlwsia.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432385994i/14950258._SX540_.png' alt=' photo ___5295375_orig_zpsklwlwsia.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Last year I read a book with a very plain orange cover, that completely did a number on me. It's a book that has stayed with me and I often think about Kate, when I read an emotional book. Apart from the main story about the beautiful Bright Side, I came away wanting to know more about Kate's best friend, Gus, because I well and truly fell for his huge heart, so this brings me to now and the book wi</span>
  <span id="freeText12871595173631183449" style="display:none">Kim Holden....... Dude........ You totally broke my heart in the most Epic way....... AGAIN!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1368.photobucket.com/user/salomax1/media/___5295375_orig_zpsklwlwsia.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432385994i/14950258._SX540_.png" alt=" photo ___5295375_orig_zpsklwlwsia.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Last year I read a book with a very plain orange cover, that completely did a number on me. It's a book that has stayed with me and I often think about Kate, when I read an emotional book. Apart from the main story about the beautiful Bright Side, I came away wanting to know more about Kate's best friend, Gus, because I well and truly fell for his huge heart, so this brings me to now and the book with the very plain black cover. <br><br>Gus's journey starts right after Kate's funeral, and to say he's a shell of his former self would be an understatement. He's drowning himself in alcohol to try and block out the pain and heartache of loosing the girl who meant the world to him. <br><br><a href="http://s1368.photobucket.com/user/salomax1/media/gus_zpswruu7qit.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432385994i/14950259._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo gus_zpswruu7qit.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For Gus it feels like life is over, but the world around him still goes on. It's time for Rook to go on tour and they need their lead singer. But with his behaviour concerning management they hire him a PA to hopefully take some of the strain. <br><br>The last thing Scout McKenzie needs is to be picking up after an Arsehole Rock Star, but it gets her away from the reality of her real life. She's a girl with secrets and scars that causes her to keep herself closed off.<br><br>I have to admit, going into this I was terrified that it could tarnish the love I have for this story, but what I got was something so unbelievably emotional, that had me consumed right from the start. I felt everything right there along side Gus and my heart broke a thousand times. Kim Holden knows how to write feelings, she knows how to capture her audience and she undoubtedly did Gus proud. <br><br>I loved how every single person was involved, how we get to catch up with everyone and see how loosing Bright Side effected each and every one of them. <br><br>This is a beautiful slow burn relationship, which teaches you not to judge a book by its cover, which fits perfect when you think of the covers for this series. I'm not usually a fan of the romance coming so far into a book, but I couldn't imagine this being done any other way. <br><br>If your after a tear jerker that makes you really feel, then pick up Bright Side followed by Gus. Pour yourself a large glass of wine, grab a large box of tissues and enjoy. </span>

<div id="review_1179249447" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1179249447" />
    <a title="C.M. Foss" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17402767-c-m-foss"><img alt="C.M. Foss" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442980031p2/17402767.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1179249447?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.M. Foss" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.M. Foss" href="/user/show/17402767-c-m-foss">C.M. Foss</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer718419672309534525">I loved Bright Side with all my heart. The book and the girl. It was so beautiful and real.<br/>But Gus. Gus stole my heart in its entirety.   <span id="freeText718419672309534525" style="display:none">I loved Bright Side with all my heart. The book and the girl. It was so beautiful and real.<br />But Gus. Gus stole my heart in its entirety. I cried more than I did for Bright Side, actually. I watched Gus in his downward spiral and I watched him grow and heal. He was so human and heart-broken and I was right there with him. <br />I felt his whole journey, and I was honored to be on it with him (and Scout).<br />I know that Bright Side changed lives, and I understand that. But it was Gus that did it for me. It (he?-- I don't even know if I'm talking about the book or him!) gave me hope and it put me back together.<br />Absolutely brilliant.<br />Well done, Kim. :)</span>

<div id="review_1655963008" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1655963008" />
    <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog"><img alt="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420222674p2/38657470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1655963008?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=we-will-rock-you">we-will-rock-you</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=audio-books">audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=library-loan">library-loan</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=6-stars">6-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1655963008" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5713615606555307938">I think <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22669832.Bright_Side__Bright_Side___1_' title='Bright Side (Bright Side, #1) by Kim Holden' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bright Side</a> is a flawless book, so even though I was curious about what happens next with Gus, I was hesitant to read this continuation of the story. I mean, how does an author successfully follow up an emotional five-star read? I have no idea, but Kim Holden makes it look easy with <i>Gus</i>.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“How do you go back to what you did before, when the other half of you is gone forever?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Gus is barely coping after his devastating loss. His pain is palpable, raw and very real, and it’s diffi</span>
  <span id="freeText5713615606555307938" style="display:none">I think <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22669832.Bright_Side__Bright_Side___1_" title="Bright Side (Bright Side, #1) by Kim Holden" rel="nofollow noopener">Bright Side</a> is a flawless book, so even though I was curious about what happens next with Gus, I was hesitant to read this continuation of the story. I mean, how does an author successfully follow up an emotional five-star read? I have no idea, but Kim Holden makes it look easy with <i>Gus</i>.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“How do you go back to what you did before, when the other half of you is gone forever?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Gus is barely coping after his devastating loss. His pain is palpable, raw and very real, and it’s difficult to see this once vibrant and carefree man struggling to find his way again. Fortunately, the majority of the book is uplifting. Gus is every bit as wonderful—funny, talented, sensitive and loyal—as he was in the previous book. He loves with his entire heart, body, and soul, and I defy you not to fall in love with him more and more.<br><br>Scout is rigid and deeply scarred emotionally. She and Gus are like oil and water, but their transformation from enemies to friends is quite heartwarming. They help support each other as both try to live a fearless life full of joy and purpose.<br><br>If you’ve read the previous book you already know that Gus has the mouth of a sailor. The cursing shouldn’t come as a surprise, but prepare yourself for some serious steam. This book is about a thousand times sexier and hotter than <i>Bright Side</i>. <br><br>Once again Kim Holden proves herself to be a superb storyteller. Grief is a process, and the story unfolds at a leisurely pace that is realistic and satisfying. There are no plot twists, no forced drama just for the sake of angst, but this book has all the feels! I couldn’t ask for a more perfect conclusion.<br><br><b>Recommended for fans of:</b><br>Emotional stories<br>Rock star romance<br>Survivors<br><br><a href="http://readingfrenzyblog.com" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458784026i/18530130.jpg" alt="Reading Frenzy Book Blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

<div id="review_1275978495" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1275978495" />
    <a title="Cristal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21745309-cristal"><img alt="Cristal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557095377p2/21745309.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1275978495?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristal" href="/user/show/21745309-cristal">Cristal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1275978495" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4977694417215707220">Originally posted on <a href='http://3lbbookblog.com/gus/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Three Little Birds Book Blog</a>.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432201636i/14909250._SY540_.jpg' width='341' height='371' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When I read Kim Holden’s books I feel like she’s writing to me and me alone. I feel connected to the story as if it’s mine. That’s her gift, and I’ll cherish it as long as she decides to write because her work makes me better. 'Bright Side' was one of the most emotional books I’ve ever read…fuck that, it was the most emotional book I’ve ever read and it made me question my life and choices more so than any other art piece has before. 'Gus' was t</span>
  <span id="freeText4977694417215707220" style="display:none">Originally posted on <a href="http://3lbbookblog.com/gus/" rel="nofollow noopener">Three Little Birds Book Blog</a>.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432201636i/14909250._SY540_.jpg" width="341" height="371" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I read Kim Holden’s books I feel like she’s writing to me and me alone. I feel connected to the story as if it’s mine. That’s her gift, and I’ll cherish it as long as she decides to write because her work makes me better. 'Bright Side' was one of the most emotional books I’ve ever read…fuck that, it was the most emotional book I’ve ever read and it made me question my life and choices more so than any other art piece has before. 'Gus' was the same. It didn’t strip me raw like 'Bright Side' did (thank Jesus, because I didn’t have anything left), but it impacted me just as deeply. It was emotionally charged, but it was truly the balm I needed for the gaping wound that 'Bright Side' left in my soul.<br><br>'Gus' was my most anticipated read of the year. I’ve been waiting for his story since I closed 'Bright Side'. The way we left him…his anguish, the sheer devastation of his grief as he faced the horrible prospect of continuing life without his soul mate, his best friend, his bright sun, his everything. To say it was heartbreaking would be a fucking gross understatement. He was a wreck, I was a wreck, it was a mess. It was amazing. So of course, I was dying for his story. I needed to see him whole again as I would a dear friend. I bonded with this character, and I ached for his happiness.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432201636i/14909251._SY540_.jpg" width="315" height="397" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>His journey was a hard one, and I was in a state of constant anxiety as I watched him battle through his grief. In the beginning of 'Gus', I ached so much for him as he made some devastating choices in order to bear the pain. His actions were reckless, but they were honest. His grief was a living, breathing thing, and it consumed his whole being. Kim Holden portrayed the total devastation that someone feels when they lose someone they love perfectly. She didn’t hold back, but then she couldn’t hold back, because we knew how much Bright Side meant to Gus, so she had to honor her memory and show the great impact that she had on the people she left behind.<br><br>Gus is an artist, so he’s a sensitive soul and he gives life everything he has, and when life hits him, every part of him is bruised. I must say, I loved this part of the story. No, I’m not into people’s pain, but c’mon, Gus is the epitome of the broken rock star, and unlike other rock star stories where you only get a hint of what they’ve been through, you know Gus’ full story, so you feel the full impact. Knowing who Gus really is makes his transformation from sweet, lovable rock star, to brooding, sexy rock god that much more amazing. Commence the swooning.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432201636i/14909252.jpg" width="302" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While Gus battled to come from under his dark cloud, he also had to deal with Scout MacKenzie. The record label assigned her as Gus’ assistant, and Gus couldn't fucking stand it. I. Loved. Scout. From the moment Gus laid eyes on her and nicknamed her Impatient, I knew that their story would be epic. He thought that she was cold and judgmental, and she thought that he was a spoiled rock star asshole. I was grinning like a damned fool. Not because I was jonesing for Gus to fall in love (I still wasn’t ready to let go of Bright Side), but because I knew that what he needed was a friend who would tell him to his face that he needed to get his shit together.<br><br>With a mix of a lot humor and tolerable emotional angst (and smoking hot sexual tension!), Holden built a friendship between Gus and Scout. They were both dealing with heartbreak and, even though they didn’t know it, their reluctant friendship helped them heal. And isn’t that just exactly what it’s all about? Kim Holden showed me once again that what is important in life is building true and honest relationships with good people. Not with perfect people, since that’s not real, but with people who look at you and see you, and still love you. People who feel your hurt and cry for you. People who try with everything they have to make you smile.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432201636i/14909253.jpg" width="317" height="390" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think that Kim Holden is that kind of person. I believe that with her writing she’s acknowledging that she sees us all and she loves us. I think she knows that we hurt, and she hurts with us. I know that she tries to make us smile, even if in order to do that, she has to make us cry first. And yes, 'Gus' will make you smile. By the end of this story, I was smiling so big and so bright. She creates these stories with these characters that are so very identifiable, so that we’ll see ourselves when we read about them, and we’ll have the courage to live to be happy too. Some might call that cheesy, but do you know what I say? Cheese is delicious.<br><br>Read 'Gus' and feel fulfilled. You don’t have to read 'Bright Side' first, because it can stand on its own, but why wouldn’t you want some Bright Side in your life. It just makes 'Gus' that much better. That’s it though, isn’t it? The pain makes the pleasure so much sweeter.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432201636i/14909254._SY540_.jpg" width="408" height="580" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Connect with <b>Three Little Birds Book Blog</b>: <br><a href="http://3lbbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ∣ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/3lbbookblog/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ∣ <a href="https://twitter.com/3lbbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4977694417215707220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText4505872208554570490" style="display:none">People, I'm going to go over board here and rate this with <br><br><b>"6 GUS stars"</b><br><br>this story deserves no less...and it was an experience I won't forget...<br><br>this was a closure I needed, it was more than enough to make me feel <b>COMPLETE</b> on several different levels...and bear with me cause I can't help it LOL but do this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434276459i/15196211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421034676ra/13312848.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and yes Gus was in my heart already from the first book <b>Bright Side</b>, he was just the one who fit in that one part of my shattered heart to fill it with hope...<br><br>and what I got from him was more - as he calls it redemption, it was a road much needed to feel whole again and to heal..to come to a point where <b>LOSS</b> is <b>NOT a LACK</b> but a <b>JOINT PART</b>, a <b>NOTION</b> that you go on <b>LIVING</b> and the memory stays with you as long as you feed it - with the fulfillment of the promise, of expectation, of hope...love can only grow on love...and that's what Scout was for Gus<br><br><b>I loved the different point of view on scars...that had a special, special meaning for me - you see, there are scars on the outside and scars on the inside, and people wear them differently...those that are NOT visible are coming out through out their actions and thoughts....but those who have them on the outside are in double danger of having been scared on the inside as well....</b><br><br>although we like to consider ourselves as being above superficial things like judging the others based solely on their appearences...we are actually failing in that department on an everyday basis...wheater we like to face it or not...<br>and GUS just completely blew me away with his actions towards Scout (who's wearing her outside scars but in fact learning to hide from people, being always in the backgrounds, in the shadows - Gus changes that!!!!)<br><br>Gus: <i>"So basically what you're saying is I should tell all the doubt to fuck off, because I'm better than I think I am?</i> <b>That <i>YOU</i> see me differently than <i>I</i> see me?"</b><br>Scout: <i>"Yes. That's exactly what I'm saying."</i><br>Gus: <i>
  <b>"That's exactly what I'm saying, too"</b>
</i><br> <b>
  <i>"You don't see the woman I see."</i>
</b><br> <b>
  <i>"Pretty girl. You're beautiful."</i>
</b> Another kiss paints another scar. <b>"Every,"</b> another kiss, <b>"thing,"</b> another kiss, <b>"about,"</b> another kiss, <b>"you,"</b> this kiss falls lower on my neck, <b>"is fucking perfect."</b><br><br><b>and that is what LOVING actually means, when LOVE actually makes sense as a feeling beyond describtion, what makes us larger than LIFE, that one moment in time, in this short life period we have, when you are MORE than you can be by making the one you love even greater...just two souls reaching out to each other in solace, in peace, in comfort, in love....</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430656024ra/14741959.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dusti, my lovely partner in crime called BR-ing, thank you for being here with me on this journey....</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4505872208554570490" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText4048344901691709703" style="display:none">I don't even know where to begin. <br />Obviously, we open with Gus, Katie's BFF, who is lost without her. He is adrift. Kim Holden takes us on a journey of grief, the road traveled by those left behind when a loved one leaves us. It's not pretty. But it's real. As a reader, I rolled through the pain with Gus, I felt it deep inside as if it were my own. I felt his torture. I hit rock bottom with him.<br />But I also rose from the ashes with him. <br />Is this book Bright Side? No, it isn't. It is the book that shows us what Bright Side meant...because doing epic isn't always easy. It's a choice. And Gus had to learn to choose...<br />There are not enough wonderful things that I can say about this book. KH is just...gah. She's amazing. The characters are so well developed and the emotion she draws us unreal. I laughed and cried repeatedly throughout. There was so much love in this book. It is a must read!!!<br />Don't miss out on this book. It is amazing!!! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18256676154917908764">5 I Only Do Epic Stars<br/><br/>Firstly you can call me Mrs Hawthorne because Gus owns my heart body and soul.<br/>I FLOVE him with everything that I am, <br/>A week later and I'm still in a funk, I'm really not ready to let go, I don't think EVER. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1433099808p8/1189682.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Going through Gus's heartache was like you were right there beside him, <br/>You felt the his pain weave throughout your whole body, and you couldn't help but just cry with him, for him.<br/>From about 4% of the Kim Holden had me on my knees , the tears flowed and I just wanted to</span>
  <span id="freeText18256676154917908764" style="display:none">5 I Only Do Epic Stars<br><br>Firstly you can call me Mrs Hawthorne because Gus owns my heart body and soul.<br>I FLOVE him with everything that I am, <br>A week later and I'm still in a funk, I'm really not ready to let go, I don't think EVER. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1433099808p8/1189682.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Going through Gus's heartache was like you were right there beside him, <br>You felt the his pain weave throughout your whole body, and you couldn't help but just cry with him, for him.<br>From about 4% of the Kim Holden had me on my knees , the tears flowed and I just wanted to crawl into the book and wrap Gus in my ams and love him forever. <br>There was a certain scene and I was hoping he wouldn't go down that certain road, no matter how much pain he was in, I wanted better for him, yes he snapped out of it but it broke my heart for half a second. But I do love how Kim bought certain things into the story because it makes you realise that people cope with things the best way they think they should at the time, even if they are hurting themselves in the process.<br>His journey to find himself again was just so beautiful to read, it wasn't fast it was slow and we needed that because he was going through so much, that if he had healed at the blink of an eye it would of took away the beauty from Bright Side and I'm so glad Kim gave us that, she broke my heart but then she healed it again over a thousand times. <br>I loved the relationship between Gus &amp; his mom, she was always his rock,<br>&amp;I'm glad she got her happy ever after she deserved it so much. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1433097073p8/1189656.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Scout I absolutely ADORED I loved her so much, <br>She was the cure Gus needed, but before that she had to heal herself, she had to go through the motions of finding who she was, what she wanted out of life and also letting herself open up to love, and when she did boy was she FIRE, Scout had a little naughty side to her that I just LOVED LOVED, but who wouldn't when you had a male like Gus, I'm telling you now I would always have my panties in my purse for that man ALWAYS ha!! <br>One other thing before I move on, what I LOVED about what Kim did with Scout's character was she wasn't jealous not in the slightest even though she knew Gus's feelings about certain things, and honestly that's what makes her one of my favourite heroines.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1433097130p8/1189658.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Witnessing Gus and Scouts relationship develop was just so magical, <br>Like Hazel Grace quoted "I fell in love the way you fall asleep, slowly, and then all at once"<br>That was Gus &amp; Scout and I loved every second, <br>Gus was one SEXY SEXY piece of HOTNESS in the bedroom &amp; outside of it,<br>it was like WOW Gus you can come and love me like that any day of the week. <br>There was one scene and the way Gus made love to Scout was just so beautiful to read, honestly when he loves he gives you his all, I swear you can FEEL every bit of that mans love all the way down to your toes.<br>God I do FLOVE him.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1433097104p8/1189657.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can keep on writing and writing about all the little things I loved about this book,<br>But then I'd be giving you EVERYTHING and that wouldn't be fair, I want you to go into this book and come out feeling the way I have felt.<br>I want you to LOVE Gus the way I do, because you don't know love until you meet this man,<br>He will capture your heart and never let it go, he will sink into your soul, and reside there for a lifetime. And I'm telling you that's all you want from him, because honestly he is EVERYTHING.<br><br>Kim Holden, my beautiful lady, <br>Thank you from the bottom of my heart for writing Gus, il love you forever for this gift.<br>Just like Kate, Gus is in my heart forever.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1433097175p8/1189659.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1542933808839535512">5+++ Beautiful, magical, earth shaking stars! <br/>Song: "Read All About It, Pt III" by Emile Sande<br/>Song: "Skinny Love" by Birdy<br/><br/>It has been a few days since I finished this amazing book and I know that no review I can write will do it any justice so my feelings are what I give to you. Also, I warn, I do not know how to write a "review" for this book wo including Bright Side as well....<br/><br/>Kim Holden has clearly perfected the art of writing, I say she is a magician/sorcerer of words...working magic with my</span>
  <span id="freeText1542933808839535512" style="display:none">5+++ Beautiful, magical, earth shaking stars! <br />Song: "Read All About It, Pt III" by Emile Sande<br />Song: "Skinny Love" by Birdy<br /><br />It has been a few days since I finished this amazing book and I know that no review I can write will do it any justice so my feelings are what I give to you. Also, I warn, I do not know how to write a "review" for this book wo including Bright Side as well....<br /><br />Kim Holden has clearly perfected the art of writing, I say she is a magician/sorcerer of words...working magic with my heart and soul, making me feel things w only words that I never imagined possible. After Bright Side I was left emotionally gutted, splayed open with the only hope left being that GUS would put me back together again. Gus was so much more than the healing balm for my heart though....Gus was a journey, and emotional roller coaster that I felt w every part of my being. <br />I love to get attached to a character/book but this series left me feeling as though I was a part of it...as if it was my life. I felt so much loss from Bright Side that I literally ached with grief and then with Gus I felt as though I was walking along side his day to day battle with grief, anger, self loathing and self destruction. I was wrapped up in his heart and his loss and inability to live wo Kate and I felt like, I too, would never be the same.<br />-Insert Scout...damaged, introvert, insecure, sad and lonely. Two unlikely people that were no doubt put together to help one another do so much more than heal. Soul mates in the least expected place who were able to show one another how to live and LOVE beyond anything they ever dreamed possible. The slow build up of Gus and Scouts relationship was perfect, he was growing as a man after a life changing loss...Scout was becoming the woman that she had lost along the way of her past.<br />I already loved GUS but I now love him so much more....I will never forget the way these 2 books made me feel, WHAT they made me feel and the lessons I was taught along the way.<br />I feel like a better person and I am forever thankful I finally put my big girl panties on and read these EPIC books!</span>

<div id="review_1106083938" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1106083938" />
    <a title="Anne OK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok"><img alt="Anne OK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505981069p2/285610.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1106083938?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne OK" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne OK" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok">Anne OK</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/285610-anne-ok?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1106083938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16152606927464157582">It’s show time and Kim Holden does EPIC! <br/><br/>After <i>Bright Star</i>, I didn’t know what to expect. The loss was just so heavy. How do you mend so many broken hearts? Well, you give Gus his story and he’ll do the rest. Of course, he had a little help from a young woman who will amaze, intrigue and definitely win your approval. Simply put, this one deserves five-stars from the get-go all the way to the last word.<br/><br/>All the emotional “feels” will once again attack your heart. Gus is more than I ever could have</span>
  <span id="freeText16152606927464157582" style="display:none">It’s show time and Kim Holden does EPIC! <br /><br />After <i>Bright Star</i>, I didn’t know what to expect. The loss was just so heavy. How do you mend so many broken hearts? Well, you give Gus his story and he’ll do the rest. Of course, he had a little help from a young woman who will amaze, intrigue and definitely win your approval. Simply put, this one deserves five-stars from the get-go all the way to the last word.<br /><br />All the emotional “feels” will once again attack your heart. Gus is more than I ever could have imagined him to be. You get the full impact of his dynamic personality in his struggles to survive the loss of the love of his life – and you’ll see his strengths as he pulls himself up and out of the darkness. He’ll win your heart without a doubt, even when you sometimes want to kick him in his mighty fine buttocks! <br /><br />I still have hopes that Kim Holden will give Keller and his little girl a story of their own as well. I would love to see their happy-ever-after down the road ten years or so. Please, Kim!<br /> <br /><br />Gus's story included so many real and genuine moments that left this reader drained at times, including some difficult periods of time, along with some very nice surprises. You might say that it took me right back to the “bright side.” Yes, Kate is there in every breath, every tear, and every smile. There is no doubt that her spirit lives on in those who loved her. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16152606927464157582" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1283094990" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1283094990" />
    <a title="Southern Belle Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26818604-southern-belle-book-blog"><img alt="Southern Belle Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456342127p2/26818604.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1283094990?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Southern Belle Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Southern Belle Book Blog" href="/user/show/26818604-southern-belle-book-blog">Southern Belle Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1283094990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10393666332280067640">That. Was. Spectacular. <br/><br/>Gus is every thing I hoped it would be, plus so much more. If such a thing can happen, I feel like my heart is smiling. I just feel so…complete. Satisfied. Fulfilled. Whatever word you want to use, Gus achieved it all. <br/><br/>I’m going to assume you know about Bright Side, and chances are pretty great that you’ve read it. I don’t need to tell you who Kate is. I don’t need to explain how a fictional character changed all of our lives or made us look at the world differently. Beca</span>
  <span id="freeText10393666332280067640" style="display:none">That. Was. Spectacular. <br /><br />Gus is every thing I hoped it would be, plus so much more. If such a thing can happen, I feel like my heart is smiling. I just feel so…complete. Satisfied. Fulfilled. Whatever word you want to use, Gus achieved it all. <br /><br />I’m going to assume you know about Bright Side, and chances are pretty great that you’ve read it. I don’t need to tell you who Kate is. I don’t need to explain how a fictional character changed all of our lives or made us look at the world differently. Because Kate, her world, and the words that Kim Holden wrote made such an impact on myself and I’m sure all of you, I had extremely high hopes for Gus. No doubt about it, Kim far exceeded my expectations.<br /><br />Like in Bright Side, Gus goes beyond just a simple love story. It’s bigger than that. It’s friendship. It’s family. It’s loyalty and support. It’s the future and the past meshing in a beautiful way. It’s…it is everything. Amidst Gus’ pain, heartbreak, and devastation that you’ll experience right along with him, he learns what’s important. While the pain lessens, memories last forever. He learns to embrace that important lesson. When he meets Scout, she changes him for the better, as does he for her. They both grow together into something magical. And hot. And funny. And… perfect. <br /><br />What I enjoyed more than anything else is how absolutely selfless Gus is. He puts everyone before himself, and you won’t be able to help falling even harder for him because of it. You’ll cry with him, laugh with him, and love with him. He’s the Gus we knew before, but you get to see what his world really entails in vivid color. Some relationships seem to make more sense than others in the books we read. His relationship with Scout is a no brainer. They are made for one another, and it’s a beautiful thing to watch unfold. They both change one another for the better. <br /><br />As I said before, it’s so much more than just a love story. While it is romantic and you will no doubt be sighing and swooning for our two main characters, the addition of so many others brings it all full circle. Gus’ love for his family shines through. You can feel how important his mother and Paxton are in particular. Keller and Stella are still large components in this story, and I couldn’t wait to see what Stella would be up to next. You get those scenes in the studio with the guys, which are always phenomenal. You’ll see familiar faces from the past. It’s just an all-around heartwarming novel, even though some parts are so incredibly bittersweet.<br /><br />Overall, this was so much greater than I even hoped it would be. Gus will satisfy your every need for the continuation of his story, but it’s just like Bright Side in the manner that you’ll rethink everything. You’ll step back and realize what’s right, what’s wrong, what’s important, and what you need to let go of. Grasp the important, don’t let go, and just do epic. My friend Clare was a beta reader, and when I asked her “Is this going to make me cry like BS did?” her response was so simple. She said to me, “If Bright Side broke your heart, Gus will put it back together.” She couldn’t have been more correct. Gus will heal your heart. Kim Holden, dude, you did it again. And you’ve brought out my love of the word Dude again, so thanks for that ☺<br /><br />&lt;3 Erin</span>
  <a data-text-id="10393666332280067640" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2242437453438190561">A complete 360 from the last book. My heart broke in the beginning but Kim was able to put it back together. I was grinning like a fool towards the end.   <span id="freeText2242437453438190561" style="display:none">A complete 360 from the last book. My heart broke in the beginning but Kim was able to put it back together. I was grinning like a fool towards the end. I had a fantastic time reliving the friendships, and meeting new ones, not to mention an unexpected love match that totally had me squeeeing--and I dont squee--ever! I was team Keller, but Gus is just beautiful. If you loved Gus in the first book, this one will reassure you why he's the ultimate dude. I loved how this book incorporated all things Kim--friends, wine, coffee, and tacos. Can't have enough tacos. Can't wait for everyone to read GUS!! Loved it!!! </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YGQn9fD8oMkfC0o70/pYyx/JS5kGz4PnHdk0tR3surnt8PlC6qtPXwIeEUVUbqilvrU3EUy0488QGsmFmZuxhw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4MoaI9Q8OhtXhD8VHhclzt9aNFAsWLwoxq8Q4iR8MQ5tXsSUzmvVjUqRZGuZg9WgfiZI2GYj3ADLbO3SoAs6MA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer5022195357679368229">Some of my favorite things: reading, writing, the two coolest guys on the planet (my husband and son), my bicycle (my husband built it for me), Facebook (I'm fairly certain it's an addiction at this point), iced coffee (hazelnut), and music (LOVE Sunset Sons, the 1975, Dredg, the xx, Balance and Composure, Teenage Bottlerocket, and 30 Seconds to Mars).   <span id="freeText5022195357679368229" style="display:none">Some of my favorite things: reading, writing, the two coolest guys on the planet (my husband and son), my bicycle (my husband built it for me), Facebook (I'm fairly certain it's an addiction at this point), iced coffee (hazelnut), and music (LOVE Sunset Sons, the 1975, Dredg, the xx, Balance and Composure, Teenage Bottlerocket, and 30 Seconds to Mars). I also love dreaming, which brings me to my next point. I have one bit of advice for anyone reading this ... follow your dreams. It's never too late. Get started today ... heck get started RIGHT NOW! I wanted to write a book 20 years ago. Instead I waited. And waited. I should've been writing. But I didn't. I don't do regrets, because the past is just that, the past. But let me tell you there's nothing in the world like achieving something you've dreamt about for years and years. So, get started. Make your dreams reality. <br />I love to hear from other readers. Send me a message or find me on Facebook (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://facebook.com/kimholdenauthor">https://facebook.com/kimholdenauthor</a>) and tell what's up in your reading world.</span>
